I booked my Z in at 8am on Monday to have the brakes examined and then Todd phoned me to suggest what work needed to be carried out. The front brakes were fine but he said new pads and rotors ( he said they could sand down the old rotors but they may squeak a bit ) were needed for the rear. I went with new rotors for around $200 more...( I hate squeaky brakes ). My wife followed me down and after a quick chat with Todd ( so we were on the same page ) I handed him the keys. I figured i would get my Z back early in the afternoon and sure enough at about 2pm Todd called to say my car was ready. 110098063328913364320< /user>
<Time>1522526154994< /Time><rate>3</rate><pics>None</pics>< Review>
I have lived on the west edge of Willow Glen for 32 years, and just found out that the Willow Glen Community Center even exists!
I do not go on the computer much, but I have overnite guests to entertain this weekend. Google popped up its name and Farmers Market for 'Nearby Events Today'.

The link to the city's website on the event gave only 'San Jose 95113' as a street address (apparently they don't know the actual street address either!), so I had to Google that too. The Farmer's Market ends in 10 minutes at 1pm. Darn.

Driving down Lincoln Ave over the years, I always just thought it was some local WG community church, not a public government building. Being retired, it is nice to know there is things going on nearby, where I do not need to contend with Traffic.

So it gets three stars for simply existing, but minus 2 for very poor community outreach.</Review>

This restaurant has a big menu with lots of selections, and it seems they do the more Chinese-style dishes better than their HK-bistro-style dishes (which is fitting to their Chinese name "Cha-Chan-Teng" Ëå∂È§êÂª≥).

Although lacking "smoothness" the hot milk tea is still acceptable, but I wouldn't order the cold one again.

The Seafood Fried Rice with XO Sauce was good, with variety of seafood--even fish!--and sufficient "wok aroma" ÈëäÊ∞£, but as with the dish from any other places, one would want bigger pieces of seafood and more xo sauce.

The two Baked Rice--Baked Pork Chop and Portuguese Chicken--both lacked flavor in The sauce, left my friends and I a lot more to desire (we only finished half of each).

Service is what one gets in a typical Chinese restaurant, so you wouldn't expect much, but the restaurant itself is spacious and open, and when my friends and I stayed for a long lunch (reunion), we didn't feel pressured to leave.<//review>

< review>
The food is good, typical spicy (not mild), friendly polite folks. The dining area is minimalistic - simple chair tables, a little on the tight side - but clean.  DId I say the food is good - their tandoori roti is excellent, the foods I have tried - saag paneer, aloo gobhi, matter paneer, aloo matter - taste like home - typical haryanwi or punjabi style of cooking.  Had egg-bhurji wrap once - that was not to my liking - too much onion, but others with me enjoyed it.  So no frills, good food kind of place - gives the impression that they do more take-out business than dine-in.</review>

< Rating>
4<//Rating>
< text>
Authentic Indian Cuisine, with a lunch buffet special and filling portions for a fair price. They actually make spicy food, which is becoming more rare to Indian restaurants throughout the SF Bay area due to complaints by surprised customers. I love spicy foods so when I discovered this cafe, I was sold. Veggie pakora is divine, and the saag paneer that my GF always orders is always savory, green, and has a very slight lemon/citrus element. The reasons I didn't give this cafe the five star is the decor seems worn, and advertisements seem a little out of character to the dining experience. Utensils/tables seem well worn as well. Register needs to be updated so the side laptop isn't necessary for the rewards. Some customers might be a little iffy on that but I've never had issues. They need a little visual/operational TLC, but the food brings us back every time.

Update: It seems like they added new colorful  lights and some curtains. Looks so much better. Excellent üëå. I added a picture so you all can see what I mean.<//text>
